
-----title
江陵 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='361fe979549e4f258e7158f972872eb7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("361fe979549e4f258e7158f972872eb7");'><span id='361fe979549e4f258e7158f972872eb7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=717&endYear=721')">717-721年</a>，1-5岁</div><div id='361fe979549e4f258e7158f972872eb7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=717&endYear=721')">717-721年</a>　岑参约生于717年（本表所标年岁均为虚拟数，非实数），居乡，5岁始读书。岑氏本宰相世家，烜赫一时，而参出生前四年，从父岑羲得罪伏诛，家族由此败落。参家世既如此，故一生仕进心切，不甘隐沦，然宦途多舛，暮景凄凉。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临汾（晋州）

-----title
登封（颍阳）
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=735')">731-735年</a>　15岁移居嵩山少室，时其父已卒，家贫，从兄受业，时与嵩洛间处士往还，作诗唱和。而实不甘隐居山野，潜怀仕进之志，诗中每露此态。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　居嵩山少室时，有诗寄王姓友人。岑参早岁诗多写山野隐居、田园风光，语多清新奇峻。作品：《丘中春卧寄王子》<div id='poem_22359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22359' class='poemTitle -----title
巩义（颍阳）

class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22691")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2523, "poem_allusion_22691")'>独往</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22691'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22691'>王生今才子<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作人）</span>，时辈咸所仰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22691'>何当见颜色，终日劳梦想。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22691'>驱车到关下，欲往阻河广。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22691'>满日徒春华，思君罢心赏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22691'>开门见太华，朝日映高掌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22691'>忽觉莲花峰，别来更如长。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22691'>无心顾微禄，有意在<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2523, "poem_sentence_6_22691")'>独往</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22691'>不负林中期，终当出尘网。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_22691_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_2_22459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22459'>置酒聊相送，青门一醉眠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=738&endYear=738')">738年</a>　往来京洛，尝于浐水客店送友人唐子。作品：《浐水东店送唐子归嵩阳》<div id='poem_22413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=740&endYear=740')">740年</a>　自河朔归来，一度客居长安，多与当时俊茂之士往来。有诗赠别郭乂。作品：《送郭乂杂言》<div id='poem_22650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>渔父</a><span class='authorDate'>（743年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22671")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22671'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22671'>扁舟沧浪叟，心与沧浪清。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22671'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22671_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=743&endYear=743')">743年</a>　岑参登第前尝隐居终南山，然并非真心归隐，实则一意求仕，但困于出仕无门，故作《感旧赋》以感伤弱冠以来数年间怀才未遇、知音难觅之苦境。<div id='poem_1367098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367098' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367098?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感旧赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（743年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_1367098")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367098_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367098'>参相门子。五岁读书。九岁属文。十五隐于嵩阳。二十献书阙下。尝自谓曰。云霄坐致。青紫俯拾。金尽裘敝。蹇而无成。岂命之过欤。国家六叶。吾门三相矣。江陵公为中书令。辅太宗。邓国公为文昌右相。辅高宗。汝南公为侍中。辅睿宗。相承宠光。继出辅弼。易曰。物不可以终泰。故受之以否。逮乎武后临朝。邓国公由是得罪。先天中。汝南公又得罪。朱轮华毂。如梦中矣。今王道休明。噫世业沦替。犹钦若前德。将施于后人。参年三十。未及一命。昔一何荣矣。今一何悴矣。直念昔者。为赋云。其辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367098_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367098'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367098'>吾门之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367098_comment'></div>世克其昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367098_comment'></div>赫矣烈祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367098_comment'></div>辅于周王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367098_comment'></div>启封受楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367098_comment'></div>佐命克商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367098_comment'></div>二千馀载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367098_comment'></div>六十馀代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367098_comment'></div>继厥美而有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367098_comment'></div>其后辟土宇于荆门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367098_comment'></div>树桑梓于棘阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367098_comment'></div>吞楚山之神秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367098_comment'></div>与汉水之灵长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367098_comment'></div>猗盛德之不陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367098_comment'></div>谅嘉声而允臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367098_comment'></div>庆延自远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367098_comment'></div>祜洽无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367098_comment'></div>自天命我唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367098_comment'></div>始灭暴隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367098_comment'></div>挺生江陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367098_comment'></div>杰出辅时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367098_comment'></div>为国之翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367098_comment'></div>斯文在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367098_comment'></div>一入麟阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367098_comment'></div>三迁凤池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367098_comment'></div>调元气以无忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367098_comment'></div>理苍生而不亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367098_comment'></div>典丝言而作则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367098_comment'></div>阐绵蕝以成规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367098_comment'></div>革亡国之前政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367098_comment'></div>赞圣代之新轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367098_comment'></div>捧尧日以云从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367098_comment'></div>扇舜风而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1367098", 1367098, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>草靡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367098_comment'></div>洋洋乎令问不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367098_comment'></div>继生邓公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367098_comment'></div>世实须才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367098_comment'></div>尽忠致君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367098_comment'></div>极武登台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367098_comment'></div>朱门复启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367098_comment'></div>相府重开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367098_comment'></div>川换新楫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367098_comment'></div>羹传旧梅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367098_comment'></div>何纠缠以相轧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367098_comment'></div>恶高门之祸来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367098_comment'></div>当其武后临朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367098_comment'></div>奸臣窃命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367098_comment'></div>百川沸腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367098_comment'></div>四国无政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367098_comment'></div>昊天降其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1367098", 1367098, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>荐瘥</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367098_comment'></div>靡风发于时令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367098_comment'></div>藉小人之荣宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367098_comment'></div>堕贤良于槛阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367098_comment'></div>苟悯怓以相蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367098_comment'></div>胡丑厉以职竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367098_comment'></div>既破我室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367098_comment'></div>又坏我门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367098_comment'></div>上帝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1367098", 1367098, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>懵懵</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367098_comment'></div>莫知我冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367098_comment'></div>众人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1367098", 1367098, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>懀懀</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367098_comment'></div>不为我言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367098_comment'></div>泣贾谊于长沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367098_comment'></div>痛屈平于湘沅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367098_comment'></div>夫物极则变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367098_comment'></div>感而遂通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367098_comment'></div>于是日光回照于覆盆之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367098_comment'></div>阳气复暖于寒谷之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367098_comment'></div>上天垂鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367098_comment'></div>佑我伯父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367098_comment'></div>为邦之杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367098_comment'></div>为国之辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367098_comment'></div>又治阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367098_comment'></div>更作霖雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367098_comment'></div>伊廊庙之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367098_comment'></div>皆祖父之旧矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367098_comment'></div>朱门不改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367098_comment'></div>画戟重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367098_comment'></div>暮出黄阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367098_comment'></div>朝趋紫宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367098_comment'></div>绣毂照路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367098_comment'></div>玉珂惊尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367098_comment'></div>列亲戚以高会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367098_comment'></div>沸歌钟于上春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367098_comment'></div>无小无大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367098_comment'></div>皆为缙绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367098_comment'></div>禺禺卬卬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367098_comment'></div>踰数十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367098_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367098_comment'></div>一心弼谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367098_comment'></div>多树纲纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367098_comment'></div>群小见丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367098_comment'></div>独醒积毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367098_comment'></div>铄于众口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367098_comment'></div>病于十指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367098_comment'></div>由是我汝南公复得罪于天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367098_comment'></div>当是时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367098_comment'></div>偪侧崩波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367098_comment'></div>苍黄反覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367098_comment'></div>去乡离土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367098_comment'></div>隳宗破族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367098_comment'></div>云雨流离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367098_comment'></div>江山放逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367098_comment'></div>愁见苍梧之云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367098_comment'></div>泣尽湘潭之竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367098_comment'></div>或投于黑齿之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1367098_comment'></div>或窜于文身之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1367098_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1367098_comment'></div>天不可问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367098_comment'></div>莫知其由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367098_comment'></div>何先荣而后悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367098_comment'></div>曷曩乐而今忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367098_comment'></div>尽世业之陵替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367098_comment'></div>念平昔之淹留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367098_comment'></div>嗟余生之不造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1367098_comment'></div>常恐堕其嘉猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367098_comment'></div>志学集其荼蓼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367098_comment'></div>弱冠干于王侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1367098_comment'></div>荷仁兄之教导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1367098_comment'></div>方励已以增修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1367098_comment'></div>无负郭之数亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1367098_comment'></div>有嵩阳之一邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1367098_comment'></div>幸逢时主之好文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1367098_comment'></div>不学沧浪之垂钩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1367098_comment'></div>我从东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1367098_comment'></div>献书西周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1367098_comment'></div>出入二郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1367098_comment'></div>蹉跎十秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1367098_comment'></div>多遭脱幅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1367098_comment'></div>累遇焚舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1367098_comment'></div>雪冻穿屦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1367098_comment'></div>尘缁敝裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1367098_comment'></div>嗟世路之其阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1367098_comment'></div>恐岁月之不留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1367098_comment'></div>眷城阙以怀归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1367098_comment'></div>将欲返云林之旧游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1367098_comment'></div>遂抚剑而歌曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1367098_comment'></div>东海之水化为田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1367098_comment'></div>北溟之鱼飞上天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1367098_comment'></div>城有时而复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1367098_comment'></div>陵有时而迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1367098_comment'></div>理固常矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1367098_comment'></div>人亦其然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1367098_comment'></div>观夫陌上豪贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1367098_comment'></div>当年高位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1367098_comment'></div>歌钟沸天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1367098_comment'></div>鞍马照地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1367098_comment'></div>积黄金以自满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1367098_comment'></div>矜青云之坐致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1367098_comment'></div>高馆招其宾朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1367098_comment'></div>重门謺其车骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1367098_comment'></div>及其高台倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1367098_comment'></div>曲池平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1367098_comment'></div>雀罗空悲其处所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1367098_comment'></div>门客肯念其平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1367098_comment'></div>已矣夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1367098_comment'></div>世路崎岖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1367098_comment'></div>孰为后图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1367098_comment'></div>岂无畴日之光荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1367098_comment'></div>何今人之弃余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1367098_comment'></div>彼乘轩而不恤尔后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1367098_comment'></div>曾不爱我之羁孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1367098_comment'></div>叹君门兮何深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1367098_comment'></div>顾盛时而向隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1367098_comment'></div>揽蕙草以惆怅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1367098_comment'></div>步衡门而踟蹰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1367098_comment'></div>强学以待知音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1367098_comment'></div>不无思达人之惠顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1367098_comment'></div>庶有望于亨衢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_166_1367098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22653'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22653'>井上桐叶雨<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作赤）</span>，灞亭卷秋风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22653'>故人适战胜，匹马归山东。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22653'>问君今年三十几，能使香名满人耳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22653'>君不见三峰直上五千仞，见君文章亦如此。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22653'>如君兄弟天下稀，雄辞健笔皆若飞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22653'>将军金印亸紫绶，御史<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_22653", 22653, "Clauses/11/Comments/1")'>铁冠</span>重<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_6_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22653'>魏侯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_22653", 22653, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>校理</span>复何如，前日人来不得书。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22653'>陆浑山下佳可赏，蓬阁闲时日应往。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22653'>自料青云未有期，谁知白发偏能长。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22653'>垆头青丝白玉瓶，别时相顾酒如倾。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22653'>摇鞭举袂忽不见，千树万树空蝉鸣。<div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22670'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22670'>君不见梁孝王脩竹园，颓墙隐辚势仍存。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22670'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22670", 22670, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>娇娥</span>曼脸成草蔓，罗帷珠帘空竹根。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22670'>大梁一旦人代改，秋月春风不相待。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22670'>池中几度雁新来，洲上千年鹤应在<span class='inlineComment2'>（梁园中有雁池、鹤洲）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22670'>万事翻覆如浮云，昔人空在今人口。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22670'>单父古来称<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1023, "poem_sentence_7_22670")'>宓生</span>，祗今为政有吾兄<span class='inlineComment2'>（家兄时宰单父）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22670'>輶轩若过梁园道，应傍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_22670", 22670, id='poem_sentence_3_22384'>独有凤皇池上客，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(196, "poem_sentence_3_22384")'>阳春</span>一曲和皆难。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22384'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_22384'><span class='label'>按：</span>
    <span class='label'>附同题诸作</span><br />　<span class='charType'>王维</span><br />绛帻鸡人送晓筹，尚衣方进翠云裘。九天阊阖开宫殿，万国衣冠拜冕旒。日色才临仙掌动，香烟欲傍衮龙浮。朝罢须裁五色诏，佩声归向凤池头。<br />
　<span class='charType'>杜甫</span><br />五夜漏声催晓箭，九重春色醉仙桃。旌旗日暖龙蛇动，宫殿风微燕雀高。朝罢香烟携满袖，诗成珠玉在挥毫。欲知世掌丝纶美①，池上于今有凤毛。<span class="small"><span class='label'>原注：</span>① 舍人先世尝掌丝纶</span><br />
　<span class='charType'>贾至</span><br />银烛熏天紫陌长，禁城春色晓苍苍。千条弱柳垂青琐，百啭流莺绕建章。剑佩声随玉墀步，衣冠身惹御炉香。共沐恩波凤池上，朝朝染翰侍君王。

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　763年正月再入长安，任职御史台。秋，任祠部员外郎。京兆府尹刘晏府中棠树降甘露，以为瑞征，有诗记之。作品：《尹相公京兆府中棠树降甘露诗》<div id='poem_22559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22559' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　766年，岁初在长安，二月，诏相国杜鸿渐为山南西道、剑南东西川副元帅，剑南西川节度使，以平蜀乱。杜表岑为职方郎中兼侍御史，同入蜀。二月至四月滞留梁州，四月南行入蜀，六月过剑门，七月抵成都。有诗酬和杜鸿渐《初发京城作》。作品：《奉和杜相公初发京城作》<div ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22553")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22553_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22553'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22553'>君家赤骠画不得，一团旋风桃花色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22553'>红缨紫鞚珊瑚鞭，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22553", 22553, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>玉鞍</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22553", 22553, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>锦鞯</span>黄金勒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22553'>请君鞲<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作鞁）</span>出看君骑，尾长窣地如红丝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22553'>自矜诸马皆不及，却忆百金新买时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22553'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_22553", 22553, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>香街</span>紫陌凤城内，满城见者谁不爱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22553'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_22553", 22553, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>扬鞭</span>骤急白汗流，弄影行骄碧蹄碎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22553'>紫髯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_22553", 22553, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>胡雏</span>金剪刀，平明剪出三鬉高。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22553'>枥上看时独意气，众中牵出偏雄豪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22553'>骑将猎向南山口，城南狐兔不复有。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22553'>草头一点疾如飞，却使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_22553", 22553, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>苍鹰</span>翻向后。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22553'>忆昨看君朝未央，鸣珂拥盖满路香。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22553'>始知边将真富贵，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_22553", 22553, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>可怜</span>人马相辉光。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22553'>男儿称意得如此，骏马长鸣北风起。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
冀州（信都）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='792f3b018fb243c1b1e27f231d79b63c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("792f3b018fb243c1b1e27f231d79b63c");'><span id='792f3b018fb243c1b1e27f231d79b63c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>，23岁</div><div id='792f3b018fb243c1b1e27f231d79b63c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　抵冀州时与王绮饮客舍，饮酣，有诗题冀州南门城楼。作品：《冀州客舍酒酣贻王绮寄题南楼》<div id='poem_22701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冀州客舍酒酣贻王绮寄题南楼<span class='inlineComment2'>（时王子欲应制举西上）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（739年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22701")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22701_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22701'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3188, "poem_allusion_22701")'>下笔不休</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22701'>夫子傲常调，诏书下徵求。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22701'>知君欲谒帝，秣马趋西周。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22701'>逸足何骎骎，美声实风流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22701'>学富赡清词，下笔不能休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22701'>君家一何盛，赫奕难为俦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22701'>伯父四五人，同时为诸侯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22701'>忆昨始相值，值君客贝丘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22701'>相看复乘兴，携手到冀州。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22701'>前日在南县，与君上北楼。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22701'>野旷不见山，白日落草头。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22701'>客舍梨花繁，深花隐鸣鸠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22701'>南邻新酒熟，有女弹箜篌。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22701'>醉后或狂歌，酒醒满离忧。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22701'>主人不相识，此地难淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_13_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_22701'>吾庐终南下，堪与王孙游。<div id='poem_sentence_14_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_22701'>何当肯相寻，澧上一孤舟。<div id='poem_sentence_15_22701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_22701'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_22701_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
浚县（黎阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7c29fc31a7aa44a3b8931bb82a57b270_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7c29fc31a7aa44a3b8931bb82a57b270");'><span id='7c29fc31a7aa44a3b8931bb82a57b270_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>，23岁</div><div id='7c29fc31a7aa44a3b8931bb82a57b270' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　过黎阳，访狄明府兄弟。作品：《临河客舍呈狄明府兄留题县南楼》<div id='poem_22628' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22628' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22628?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临河客舍呈狄明府兄留题县南楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（739年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22628")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22628_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22628'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22628'>黎阳城南雪正飞，黎阳渡头人未归<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作渡口人渡稀）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22628'>河边酒家堪寄宿，主人小女能缝衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22628'>故人高卧黎阳县，一别三年不相见。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22628'>邑中雨雪偏着时，隔河东郡人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_22628", 22628, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>遥羡</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22628'>邺都唯见古时丘，漳水还如旧日流。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22628'>城上望乡应不见，朝来好是懒登楼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22628'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22628_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title

id='poem_sentence_0_22542'>骊姬北原上，闭骨已千秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22542'>浍水日东注，恶名终不流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22542'>献公恣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_22542", 22542, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>耽惑</span>，视子如仇雠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22542'>此事成<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6204, "poem_sentence_3_22542")'>蔓草</span>，我来逢古丘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22542'>蛾眉山月苦，蝉鬓野云愁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22542'>欲吊二公子，横汾无轻舟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22542'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22542_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
大荔（朝邑）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e54f83192014441ba30cf21e629f80dd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e54f83192014441ba30cf21e629f80dd");'><span id='e54f83192014441ba30cf21e629f80dd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>，29岁</div><div id='e54f83192014441ba30cf21e629f80dd' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
淇县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7dac6380808442f5b33ec2082930df69_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7dac6380808442f5b33ec2082930df69");'><span id='7dac6380808442f5b33ec2082930df69_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>　尝往游淇上，淇上友人以诗赠岑参，参亦以诗答之。作品：《敬酬杜华淇上见赠兼呈熊曜》<div id='poem_22674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_22674'>祗曾效<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作为）</span>一官，今已年四十。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22674'>是君同时者，已有尚书郎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22674'>怜君独未遇，淹泊在他乡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22674'>我从京师来，到此喜相见。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22674'>共论穷途事，不觉泪满面。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22674'>忆昨癸未岁，吾兄自江东。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22674'>得君江湖诗，骨气凌谢公。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22674'>县楼压春岸，戴胜鸣花枝。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22674'>吾徒在舟中，纵酒兼弹棋。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22674'>三月犹未还，寒愁满春草。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22674'>赖蒙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_22674", 22674, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>瑶华</span>赠，讽咏慰怀抱。<div id='poem_sentence_13_22674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_22674'></div><div -----title
礼泉（醴泉）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f16e99f77b1748f590695970aeadf3c7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f16e99f77b1748f590695970aeadf3c7");'><span id='f16e99f77b1748f590695970aeadf3c7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>，29岁</div><div id='f16e99f77b1748f590695970aeadf3c7' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>进士及第次年始解褐，授右内率府兵曹参军，居长安，半官半隐。与杜明府宴饮，有诗纪之。作品：《春日醴泉杜明府承恩五品宴席上赋诗》<div id='poem_22410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春日醴泉杜明府承恩五品宴席上赋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（745年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22410")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22410_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22410'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1683, "poem_allusion_22410")'>凫舄</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22410'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22410'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1683, "poem_sentence_0_22410")'>凫舄</span>旧称仙，鸿私降自天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22410'>青袍移草色，朱绶夺花然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22410'>邑里雷仍震，台中星欲悬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22410'>吾兄此栖棘，因得贺初筵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22410'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; 户县（长安）

-----title
天水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='325d2295614f4a7db031b47ef39b0a9f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("325d2295614f4a7db031b47ef39b0a9f");'><span id='325d2295614f4a7db031b47ef39b0a9f_link' 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>749年冬，岑参时33岁，入佐高仙芝幕府。西行由阳关一线至安西，途经陇山时有诗寄友人宇文判官。作品：《初过陇山途中呈宇文判官》<div id='poem_22606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_22606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22606'>一驿过一驿，驿骑如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_22606", 22606, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>星流</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22606'>平明发咸阳，暮及陇山头。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22606'>陇水不可听，呜咽令人愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22606'>沙尘扑马汗，雾露凝貂裘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22606'>西来谁家子，自道新封侯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22606'>前月发安西，路上无停留。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22606'>都护犹未到，来时在西州。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22606'>十日过沙碛，终朝风不休。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22606'>马走碎石中，四蹄皆血流。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22606'>万里奉王事，一身无所求。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22606'>也知塞垣苦，岂为妻子谋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22606'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_22606", 22606, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>山口</span>月欲出，先照关城楼。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22606'>溪流与松风，静夜相飕飗<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作飕）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22606'>别家<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作来）</span>赖归梦，山塞多离忧。<div id='poem_sentence_15_22606'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_22606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_22606'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(22606)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至陇头有诗纪之。作品：《经陇头分水》<div id='poem_22323' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22323' -----title
酒泉
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3241449d54de41a1890175a0140d3df1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3241449d54de41a1890175a0140d3df1");'><span id='3241449d54de41a1890175a0140d3df1_link' id='poem_sentence_0_22331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22331'>马上相逢无纸笔，凭君<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22331", 22331, 敦煌

张掖

id='poem_sentence_0_22578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22578'>高堂满地红氍毹，试舞一曲天下无。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 临潭（洮州）

color: gray;'>▪</span>游临洮龙兴寺，与寺中玄上人同咏花木。作品：《临洮龙兴寺玄上人院同咏青木香丛》<div id='poem_22401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临洮龙兴寺玄上人院同咏青木香丛</a><span class='authorDate'>（751年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22401")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22401'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22401'>移根自远方，种得在僧房。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22401'>六月花新吐，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22401", 22401, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>三春</span>叶已长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22401'>抽茎高锡杖，引影到绳床。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22401'>只为能除疾，倾心向药王。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22401'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22401_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4ba05bc4a40e466bb7c2ddc4913c6a31_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ba05bc4a40e466bb7c2ddc4913c6a31");'><span id='4ba05bc4a40e466bb7c2ddc4913c6a31_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年</a>，38岁</div><div id='4ba05bc4a40e466bb7c2ddc4913c6a31' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; id='poem_sentence_1_22623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22623'>戍楼西望烟尘黑，汉兵屯在轮台北。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_22399'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22399'>轮台风物异，地是古单于。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22399'>蕃书文字别，胡俗语音殊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22399'>愁见流沙北，天西海一隅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22399'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年8月</a>　八月，在轮台，武判官归京，有诗送行。作品：《白雪歌送武判官归京》<div id='poem_22579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_5_22579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22579'>纷纷暮雪下辕门，风掣红旗冻不翻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>　在北庭，见优钵罗花而作歌，兼感怀身世。作品：《优钵罗花歌并序》<div id='poem_22583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22583?labeling=true' target='_blank'>优钵罗花歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（756年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22583")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22583_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_22583'>参尝读佛经，闻有优钵罗花，目所未见。天宝庚申岁，参忝大理评事，摄监察御史，领伊西北庭度支副使。自公多暇，乃于府庭内，栽树种药，为山凿池，婆娑乎其间，足以寄傲。交河小吏有献此花者，云得之于天山之南，其状异于众草，势巃嵷如冠弁。嶷然上耸，生不傍引；攒花中折（攒花中拆），骈叶外包；异香腾风，秀色媚景。因赏而叹曰：「尔不生于中土，僻在遐裔，使牡丹价重，芙蓉誉高，惜哉！」夫天地无私，阴阳无偏，各遂其生，自物厥性，岂以偏地而不生乎，岂以无人而不芳乎？适此花不遭小吏，终委诸山谷，亦何异怀才之士，未会明主，摈于林薮邪！因感而为歌，歌曰：</div><div id='poem_preface_22583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22583'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22583'>白山南，赤山北，其间有花人不识。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22583'>绿茎碧叶好颜色，叶六瓣，花九房，夜掩朝开多异香，何不生彼中国兮生西方？<div id='poem_sentence_1_22583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22583'>移根在庭，媚我公堂，耻与众草之为伍，何亭亭而独芳？<div id='poem_sentence_2_22583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22583'>何不为人之所赏兮？<div id='poem_sentence_3_22583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22583'>深山穷谷委严霜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22583'>吾窃悲阳关道路长，曾不得献于君王。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_22583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_22583'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>，40岁</div><div id='f46a7e94b0aa42239927c55a537206f9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，在北庭，郭司马赴任伊吾郡，有诗送行，并告示李明府。作品：《送郭司马赴伊吾郡请示李明府》<div id='poem_22462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22462?labeling=true' 凤翔

id='poem_sentence_2_22596'>胡兵夺长安，宫殿生野草。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22596'>伤心五陵树，不见二京道。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22371'>晚岁宦情薄，行军欢宴疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 城固

-----title
汉中（梁州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='588acc3cfae047cd851402db32b8c6f5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("588acc3cfae047cd851402db32b8c6f5");'><span id='588acc3cfae047cd851402db32b8c6f5_link' 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，入蜀途经梁州，有诗赠张献诚。作品：《过梁州奉赠张尚书大夫公》<div id='poem_22601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22601?labeling=true' id='poem_content_22601'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22601'>汉中二良将，今昔各一时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22601'>韩信此登坛，尚书复来斯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22601'>手把<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_22601", 22601, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>铜虎符</span>，身总丈人师。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22601'>错落北斗星，照耀黑水湄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22601'>英雄若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_22601", 22601, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>神授</span>，大材济时危。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22601'>顷岁遇雷云，精神感灵祇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22601'>勋业振青史，恩德继鸿私。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22601'>羌虏昔未平，华阳积僵尸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22601'>人烟绝墟落，鬼火依城池。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22601'>巴汉空水流，褒斜惟鸟飞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22601'>自公布德政，此地生光辉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22601'>百堵创里闾，千家恤茕嫠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22601'>层城重鼓角，甲士如熊罴。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22601'>坐啸风自调，行春雨仍随。<div id='poem_sentence_13_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_22601'>芃芃麦苗长，蔼蔼桑叶肥。<div id='poem_sentence_14_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_22601'>浮客相与来，群盗不敢窥。<div id='poem_sentence_15_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_22601'>何幸承嘉惠，小年即相知。<div id='poem_sentence_16_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_22601'>门传大夫印，世拥上将旗。<div id='poem_sentence_22_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_22601'>别有<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(680, "poem_sentence_25_22601")'>弹冠</span>士，希君无见遗。<div id='poem_sentence_25_22601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_22601'></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22544'>与时忽开闭，作固或顺逆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22544'>磅礴跨岷峨，<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_8_22544'>星当觜参分，地处西南僻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22544'>陡觉烟景殊，杳将华夏隔。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22544'>刘氏昔颠覆，公孙曾败绩。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22544'>始知德不脩，恃此险何益。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22544'>相公总师旅，远近罢金革。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22544'>杜母来何迟，蜀人应更惜。<div id='poem_sentence_13_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_22544'>暂回丹青虑，少用开济策。<div id='poem_sentence_14_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_22544'>二友华省郎，俱为幕中客。<div id='poem_sentence_15_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_22544'>良筹佐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_22544", 22544, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>戎律</span>，精理皆硕画。<div id='poem_sentence_16_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_22544'>高文出诗骚，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_22544", 22544, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>奥学</span>穷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_22544", 22544, "Clauses/35/Comments/1")'>讨赜</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_22544'>圣朝无外户，寰宇被德泽。<div id='poem_sentence_18_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_22544'>四海今一家，徒然剑门石。<div id='poem_sentence_19_22544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_22544'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_22544_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title

id='poem_sentence_11_22678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　在嘉州，登青衣山，访惠净上人居所，题诗以识其事，并呈杨炎。作品：《上嘉州青衣山中峰题惠净上人幽居寄兵部杨郎中并序》<div id='poem_22547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上嘉州青衣山中峰题惠净上人幽居寄兵部杨郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22547")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22547_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_22547'>青衣之山，在大江之中，屹然迥绝，崖壁苍峭，周广七里，长波四匝。有惠净上人，庐于其颠，唯绳床竹杖而已。恒持《莲花经》，十年不下山。予自公浮舟，聊一登眺。友人夏官弘农杨侯，清谈之士也，素工为文，独立于世，与余有方外之约，每多独往之意。今者幽躅胜概，叹不得与此公俱。爰命小吏，刮磨石壁以识其事，乃诗以达杨友尔。</div><div id='poem_preface_22547_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22547'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(923, class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22481'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22481'>水路东连楚，人烟北接巴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22481'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22481", 22481, id='poem_sentence_4_22481'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年</a>　在嘉州，观郡府壁画云片，有诗。作品：《咏郡斋壁画片云》<div id='poem_22382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>咏郡斋壁画片云<span class='inlineComment2'>（得归字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（768年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22382'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22382'>云片何人画，尘侵粉色微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22382'>丹青忽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_22382", 22382, id='poem_sentence_4_22382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年</a>　居蜀中，江行遇梅花，有诗。作品：《江行遇梅花之作》<div id='poem_22593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江行遇梅花之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（768年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22593")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22593'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22593'>江畔梅花白如雪，使我思乡肠欲绝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22593'>摘得一枝在手中，无人远向金闺说。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22593'>愿得青鸟衔此花，西飞直送到我家。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22593'>胡姬正在临窗下，独织留黄浅碧纱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22593'>此鸟衔花胡姬前，胡姬见花知我怜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22593'>千说万说由不得，一夜抱花空馆眠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22593'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_22593'><span class='label'>按：</span>（见伯二五五五卷，转录自《文献》十三辑廖立《敦煌残卷岑诗辨》）（〖1〗李嘉言《岑诗系年》云：「案岑参江陵人，而足迹不及江陵以东。此曰：『西飞直送到吾家』，其非岑作明矣。」〖2〗廖立云：「今覈对胶片，此诗题下署名为岑参〖原字作𠫭〗，不知何故《系年》未提此点。」「诗中所言胡姬，恐怕也是寄托之辞，勿须考證岑参家中是否真有一个胡姬。这是写诗，不是写史，香草美人，均非实指。《江行》为岑参之作，似勿须多辨。」）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_22593_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年7月</a>　768年七月，自嘉州罢官东归，行舟至泥溪，有诗。作品：《东归发犍为至泥溪舟中作》<div id='poem_sentence_0_22564'>前日解侯印，泛舟归山东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22564'>平旦发犍为，逍遥信回风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22564'>七月江水大，沧波涨秋空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22564'>复有峨眉僧，诵经在舟中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22564'>夜泊防虎豹，朝行逼鱼龙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22564'>一道鸣迅湍，两边走连峰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22564'>忆昨在西掖，复曾入南宫。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22564'>日出朝圣人，端笏陪群公。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22564'>不意今弃置，何由豁心胸。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22564'>吾当海上去，且学乘桴翁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
宜宾（戎州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='24064ba8795e4c139c9f4b580012a200_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("24064ba8795e4c139c9f4b580012a200");'><span id='24064ba8795e4c139c9f4b580012a200_link' id='poem_sentence_0_22613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22613'>杀人无昏晓，尸积填江湾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22613'>饿虎衔髑髅，饥乌啄心肝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22613'>腥裛滩草死，血流江水殷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22613'>夜雨风萧萧，鬼哭连楚山。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_22625' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22625?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青山峡口泊舟怀狄侍御</a><span class='authorDate'>（768年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22625")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22625_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22625'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2368, "poem_allusion_22625")'>傅说羹</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22625_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22625'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22625'>峡口秋水壮，沙边且停桡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22625'>奔涛振石壁，峰势如动摇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22625'>九月芦花新，弥令客心焦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22625'>谁念在江岛，故人满天朝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22625'>无处豁心胸，忧来醉能销。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22625'>往来巴山道，三见秋草彫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22625'>狄生新相知，才调凌云霄。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22625'>赋诗析造化，入幕生风飙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22625'>把笔判甲兵，战士不敢骄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22625'>皆云梁公后，遇鼎还能调。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22625'>离别倏经时，音尘殊寂寥。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22625'>何当见夫子，不叹乡关遥。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22625'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_22625_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，自嘉州东归，沿长江东行，泊舟，发思古之，有诗。作品：《楚夕旅泊古兴》<div id='poem_22683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楚夕旅泊古兴</a><span class='authorDate'>（768年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14000, "唐", "岑参", "poem_title_22683")'>岑参</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22683'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22683'>独鹤唳江月，孤帆凌楚云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22683'>秋风冷萧瑟，芦荻花纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22683'>忽思湘川老，欲访云中君。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22683'>骐驎息悲鸣，愁见豺虎群。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22683'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22683_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
